<div class="mf-section-0" id="mf-section-0"> 
<p>Need to take a screenshot on your Windows PC? Whether you want to <a href="/Take-a-Screenshot-of-the-Entire-Screen" title="Take a Screenshot of the Entire Screen">capture the full screen</a> or just one window or area, there are several quick and easy ways to take screenshots in Windows 10, Windows 11, and Windows 8. Taking a screenshot is a little different on each version of Windows, but this wikiHow article will teach you how to <a href="/Use-Keyboard-Shortcuts" title="Use Keyboard Shortcuts">use keyboard shortcuts</a> (including the Print Screen key), the Snipping Tool, and the Xbox Game Bar to screen capture any area of your Windows desktop.
</p>
</div>

<div class="headline_container "><div class="headline_info"><h2 class="section-heading" onclick="javascript:mfTempOpenSection(1)">
<div class="mw-ui-icon mw-ui-icon-element indicator"></div>
<span class="mw-headline" id="Taking-a-Screenshot-in-Windows">Taking a Screenshot in Windows</span>
</h2></div></div>
<div id="takingascreenshotinwindows" class="section_text">
<p>Press the <b>Windows</b> + <b>Print Screen</b> keys at the same time to capture the entire screen. You'll find the image in the <b>Screenshots</b> folder inside the <b>Pictures</b> folder. To screenshot just one area of the screen, press <b>Windows Key</b> + <b>Shift</b> + <b>S</b> to use the Snipping Tool.
</p>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="mf-section-1 collapsible-block" id="mf-section-1">

</div>

<div class="headline_info">
<div class="method_label">Method 1 of 8:</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Take-a-Quick-Full-Screen-Screenshot">Take a Quick Full Screen Screenshot</span></h3>
</div>
<a class="large_pdf_link pdf_link  disabled  pdf_link_steps  " href="#">
	
	<img class="pdf_link-img" loading="lazy" src="/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg" alt="PDF download" width="150" height="150">
	<span class="pdfText">Download Article</span>

<div id="steps_1" class="section_text">
<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-00">
<a name="step_1_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg" class="image"><picture id="9540e36fd9c06096747fa6ae5364c021"><source type="image/webp" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="546" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/96/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg.webp 460w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="546" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/96/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" srcset="/images/thumb/9/96/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" srcset="/images/thumb/9/96/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg 728w"></source><img alt="Step 1 Go to the screen that you want to capture." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/96/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="345" priority="high" onload="WH.performance.clearMarks('image1_rendered'); WH.performance.mark('image1_rendered');"><script>WH.performance.clearMarks('image1_rendered'); WH.performance.mark('image1_rendered');</script></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/9\/96\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/9\/96\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-1-Version-12.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Go to the screen that you want to capture.</b> When you screenshot your entire screen, everything that's open will be captured in your screenshot. Be sure to close any windows you don't want open.<sup id="_ref-1" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 1"><a href="#_note-1">[1]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_1" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>This method will quickly capture everything on your screen and save the image to your PC. Once you've saved the screenshot, you can <a href="/Edit-a-Screenshot" title="Edit a Screenshot">edit it</a> or share it with anyone.</li></ul>
<script>WH.performance.mark('step1_rendered');</script>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_1"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-01">
<a name="step_1_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-2-Version-9.jpg" class="image"><picture (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Find the <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode"></span> Print Screen</kbd></b></span> key on your keyboard.</b> The Print Screen key is often found on the upper-right side of the keyboard, not counting the numeric keypad.<sup id="_ref-2" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 2"><a href="#_note-2">[2]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_2" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>The Print Screen key will usually be abbreviated to "PrtSc" or something similar.</li>
<li>If your keyboard doesn't have a Print Screen key, use the Snipping Tool on <a href="#Use-Snipping-Tool-.28Windows-10.2C-8.1.2C-and-7.29">Windows 10</a> or <a href="#Use-Snipping-Tool-.28Windows-11.29">Windows 11</a>.<sup id="_ref-3" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 3"><a href="#_note-3">[3]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_3" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>  You can also use the On-Screen Keyboard and locate the PrtScn button beneath the Insert button.</li>
</ul>

screenshot." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/ae/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-3-Version-10.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-3-Version-10.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="342" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/a\/ae\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-3-Version-10.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-3-Version-10.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/a\/ae\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-3-Version-10.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-3-Version-10.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":342,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":541,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">3</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Take your screenshot.</b> You have two options for capturing your entire screen: 
<ul>
<li>
<b>Instantly save the screenshot as an image:</b> Press the <b>Windows key</b> and the <b>PrtSc</b> keys at the same time. This saves your screenshot as a PNG file to the <b>Screenshots</b> folder in your <b>Pictures</b> folder. On most keyboards, the Windows key is located in the bottom left corner on the same row as the spacebar. Upon pressing this key combination, the screen may dim briefly to indicate that the screenshot was captured.</li>
<li>
<b>Copy the screenshot so you can paste it:</b> Press the <b>Print Screen</b> key alone to copy the screen to your PC's clipboard. You can then paste the copied screenshot into a document, email message, or social media post by right-clicking the desired location and selecting <b>Paste</b>.</li>
<li>With some Windows laptops or keyboards, you will need to hold down the <b>Fn</b> key as you press the <b>Print Screen</b> key.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_3"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-03">
<a name="step_1_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg" class="image"><picture id="bae01b1c65922320b440bfc8d6f67c5e"><source type="image/webp" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="541" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/5/59/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg.webp 460w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="541" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/5/59/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="541" srcset="/images/thumb/5/59/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="541" srcset="/images/thumb/5/59/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg 728w"></source><img alt="Step 4 Find the screenshot." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/5/59/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="342" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/5\/59\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/5\/59\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-4-Version-10.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":342,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":541,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">4</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Find the screenshot.</b> If you used <b>Windows key</b> + <b>Print Screen</b> to capture the screenshot, follow these steps to <a href="/Find-Screenshots-on-PC" title="Find Screenshots on PC">find the file</a>:<sup id="_ref-4" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 4"><a href="#_note-4">[4]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden id="ts_popup_4" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup> 
<ul>
<li>Open File Explorer by pressing <b>Windows key + E</b> on your keyboard.</li>
<li>If you see a folder called <b>Pictures</b> in the left panel, click it. If not, click <b>This PC</b>, and then double-click the <b>Pictures</b> folder.</li>
<li>Double-click the <b>Screenshots</b> folder.</li>
<li>Each screenshot you take is labeled "Screenshot (number)." Depending on the version of Windows you're using, the file name will either end with a number that corresponds with the number of screenshots you've taken, or the date and time at which you captured the screenshot.</li>
<li>If you can't find your screenshot, try using the Snipping Tool instead. See <a href="#Use-Snipping-Tool-.28Windows-11.29">Snipping Tool (Windows 11)</a> or <a href="#Use-Snipping-Tool-.28Windows-10.2C-8.1.2C-and-7.29">Snipping Tool (Windows 10 and earlier)</a>.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Take-a-One-Window-Screenshot">Take a One-Window Screenshot</span></h3>
</div>
<a class="large_pdf_link pdf_link  disabled  pdf_link_steps  " href="#">

<li id="step-id-14">
<a name="step_2_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-5-Version-11.jpg" class="image"><picture <div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Click the window you want to capture.</b> If you only want to screenshot a single window, click anywhere on the window you want to capture. Make sure the window is in front of all your other windows.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_5"></div>
</li>

<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Hold down <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Alt</kbd></b></span> and press <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode"></span> PrtScr</kbd></b></span>.</b> This copies an image of the window to the clipboard.<sup id="_ref-5" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 5"><a href="#_note-5">[5]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_5" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Expert Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name"></span>
			<a class="ts_expert_link" href="/Author/Ken-Colburn"><span class="ts_expert_image"><picture><source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/0/0a/Ken_Colburn.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Ken_Colburn.png.webp"></source><img src="/images/thumb/0/0a/Ken_Colburn.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Ken_Colburn.png" alt="Ken Colburn" loading="lazy" width="30" height="30" style="max-width: 30px"></picture></span>Ken Colburn<br><span class="ts_blurb">Consumer Electronics Expert</span></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>You will not see any confirmation that the screenshot has been taken.</li>
<li>On some Windows keyboards, you will need to also hold down the <b>Fn</b> key when you use <a href="/Take-a-Screen-Shot-(Screen-Capture)" title="Take a Screen Shot (Screen Capture)">print screen</a>.</li>
<li>If your keyboard doesn't have a Print Screen key, use the Snipping Tool on <a href="#Use-Snipping-Tool-.28Windows-10.2C-8.1.2C-and-7.29">Windows 10</a> or <a href="#Use-Snipping-Tool-.28Windows-11.29">Windows 11</a>.</li>
</ul>

<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">3</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Open Paint.</b> This program comes installed on all Windows computers.<sup id="_ref-6" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 6"><a href="#_note-6">[6]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_6" style="display: none;">

</span>
</sup> To open it:
<ul>
<li>Press the <b>Windows key</b> and type <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">paint</kbd>.</li>
<li>Click <b>Paint</b>.</li>
</ul>

srcset="/images/thumb/c/cd/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-9.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-9.jpg 728w"></source><img alt="Step 4 Press Ctrl+V to paste the screenshot." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/cd/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-9.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-9.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="347" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/c\/cd\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-9.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-9.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/c\/cd\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-9.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-9.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":347,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":549,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">4</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Press <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">V</kbd></b></span> to paste the screenshot.</b> You will now see your one-window screenshot in the Paint window.<sup id="_ref-7" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 7"><a href="#_note-7">[7]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_7" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>You can also paste the screenshot into other programs, such as Word, or the body of an email. Open the program you want to paste the image into and press <b>Ctrl</b> + <b>V</b>.</li>
<li>Alternatively, you can paste the screenshot into any open document, email, or other area using this shortcut.</li>
<li>If your screenshot doesn't appear, try using the Snipping Tool instead. See <a href="#Use-Snipping-Tool-.28Windows-11.29">Snipping Tool (Windows 11)</a> or <a href="#Use-Snipping-Tool-.28Windows-10.2C-8.1.2C-and-7.29">Snipping Tool (Windows 10 and earlier)</a>.<sup id="_ref-8" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 8"><a href="#_note-8">[8]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_8" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_8"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-18">

460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="549" srcset="/images/thumb/2/2c/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-4.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-4.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="549" screenshot as an image." class="whcdn" width="460" height="347" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/2\/2c\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-4.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-4.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/2\/2c\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-4.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-4.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":347,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":549,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">5</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Save your screenshot as an image.</b> Click <b>File</b>, click <b>Save</b>, enter a file name, click a location on the left side of the page, and click <b>Save</b>.
<ul><li>You can change the screenshot's file type by clicking the "Save as type" drop-down box at the bottom of the window and then clicking a different format (e.g., <b>JPEG</b>) in the drop-down menu.</li></ul>
</div>

<span id="Use-Snipping-Tool-(Windows-11)"></span><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Use-Snipping-Tool-.28Windows-11.29">Use Snipping Tool (Windows 11)</span></h3>
</div>
<a class="large_pdf_link pdf_link  disabled  pdf_link_steps  " href="#">

<li id="step-id-29">
<a name="step_3_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-10-Version-12.jpg" class="image"><picture <div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Open the Snipping Tool.</b> The Windows 11 Snipping Tool makes it incredibly easy to capture and edit full-screen, partial-screen, and single-window screenshots. To access Snipping Tool, press the <b>Windows key</b>, type <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">snip</kbd>, and click <b>Snipping Tool</b>.<sup id="_ref-9" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 9"><a href="#_note-9">[9]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_9" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup> 
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_10"></div>
</li>

<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Select a screenshot mode.</b> Click the <b>Snipping Mode</b> menu (the square with a plus (+) at its bottom-right corner), then choose an option:
<ul>
<li>
<b>Rectangle:</b> Let's you capture any part of the screen by drawing a rectangle around an area.</li>
<li>
<b>Window:</b> Allows you to capture an individual window without getting anything else in the screenshot.</li>
<li>
<b>Full screen:</b> Captures everything on the screen.</li>
<li>
<b>Freeform:</b> Lets you draw any shape around an area of the screen to take a screenshot.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_11"></div>

<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">3</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Click <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><span class="nowrap" title="This is not a clickable button; it illustrates the button one should find." style="font-family:Lucida Sans Unicode,Lucida Grande,sans-serif;font-size:14px;padding:0em 1em; border:1px solid; border-color:#AAA #555 #555 #AAA; -moz-border-radius: 4px; -webkit-border-radius: 4px; border-radius: 4px; background-color: #F2F2F2; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #FCFCFC, #E0E0E0); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #FCFCFC, #E0E0E0); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #FCFCFC, #E0E0E0); background-image: linear-gradient(top, #FCFCFC, #E0E0E0);">+ New</span></b></span>.</b> It's at the top-left corner of Snipping Tool.<sup id="_ref-10" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 10"><a href="#_note-10">[10]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden id="ts_popup_10" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>

type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/7\/7a\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-11.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-11.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/7\/7a\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-11.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-13-Version-11.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"<div (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">4</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Capture your screenshot.</b><sup id="_ref-11" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 11"><a href="#_note-11">[11]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_11" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>In <b>Rectangle</b> mode, click and drag a rectangle around the desired area to instantly capture a screenshot.</li>
<li>In <b>Window</b> mode, click the window you want to capture to take the screenshot.</li>
<li>In <b>Full screen</b> mode, the entire screen will instantly capture.</li>
<li>In <b>Freeform</b> mode, draw an outline around the part of the screen you want to capture.</li>
<li>You can also delay the screenshot capture by a few seconds using the stopwatch menu at the top of Snipping Tool.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_13"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-213">
<a name="step_3_5" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-6.jpg" class="image"><picture 460w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="546" 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" srcset="/images/thumb/7/7e/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-6.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-6.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source Snipping Tool icon in the taskbar to view your screenshot." class="whcdn" width="460" height="345" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/7\/7e\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-6.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-6.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/7\/7e\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-6.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-14-Version-6.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">5</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Click the Snipping Tool icon in the taskbar to view your screenshot.</b> A preview of the screenshot should appear on its own. If it doesn't, click the scissors in the toolbar at the bottom of the screen to preview it now. 
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_14"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-214">
<a name="step_3_6" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-(Draft)-Step-15.jpg" class="image"><picture 460w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="546" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/f4/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-15.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-15.jpg 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" srcset="/images/thumb/f/f4/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-15.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-15.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source your screenshot (optional)." class="whcdn" width="460" height="345" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script <div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">6</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Edit your screenshot (optional).</b> Use the tools at the top of the window to edit your screenshot if you'd like. Hover your cursor over the icons to see what each tool does.
<ul>
<li>To crop a screenshot, select the Crop tool, then select the part of the screenshot you want to keep.</li>
<li>Use the pen tool to write or draw on the screenshot. This is helpful if you need to redact something.</li>
<li>You can use the highlighter to bring attention to a certain area, or the eraser tool to erase any additions you've made.</li>
<li>Use the Shapes tool to draw shapes, like a circle around text or an arrow.</li>
<li>To edit your screenshot further, click <b>Edit in Paint</b> at the top-right corner to open it in the Paint app.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_15"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-215">
<a name="step_3_7" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-(Draft)-Step-16.jpg" class="image"><picture 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" srcset="/images/thumb/c/c6/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-16.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-16.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source your screenshot." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c6/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-16.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-16.jpg" <div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">7</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Save your screenshot.</b> Now that you've taken a screenshot, you can save it easily:<sup id="_ref-12" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 12"><a href="#_note-12">[12]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_12" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>Click the disk icon at the top.</li>
<li>Select a location to save your screenshot.</li>
<li>Name your file and click <b>Save</b>.</li>
<li>Alternatively, click the Copy icon at the top-right to copy the screenshot to your clipboard. This makes it easy to paste the screenshot into any open app or document.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_16"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-216">

(screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">8</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Use the Snipping Tool shortcut in the future.</b> Now that you know how to use Snipping Tool, you can use this handy shortcut next time you want to take a screenshot: <b>Windows key</b> + <b>Shift</b> + <b>S</b>.<sup id="_ref-13" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 13"><a href="#_note-13">[13]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden id="ts_popup_13" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>When you use the keyboard shortcut, you'll see a smaller Snipping Tool at the top of the screen. Each icon on the Snipping Tool indicates a different screenshot typeRectangle, Window, Full screen, and Freeform modes. Click the mode you'd like to use, then capture your screenshot.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_17"></div>
</li>

<div class="headline_info">
<div class="method_label">Method 4 of 8:</div>
<span id="Use-Snipping-Tool-(Windows-10,-8.1,-and-7)"></span><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Use-Snipping-Tool-.28Windows-10.2C-8.1.2C-and-7.29">Use Snipping Tool (Windows 10, 8.1, and 7)</span></h3>
</div>
<a class="large_pdf_link pdf_link  disabled  pdf_link_steps  " href="#">

	<span class="pdfText">Download Article</span>

<div id="steps_4" class="section_text">
<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-317">
<a name="step_4_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg" class="image"><picture id="a913b5790f1f8bd6469f5d4ca9db583a"><source type="image/webp" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="544" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d1/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg.webp 460w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="544" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d1/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="544" srcset="/images/thumb/d/d1/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="544" srcset="/images/thumb/d/d1/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg 728w"></source><img alt="Step 1 Open the Snipping..." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d1/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="344" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/d\/d1\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/d\/d1\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-15-Version-4.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":344,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":544,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Open the <a href="/Use-a-Snipping-Tool" title="Use a Snipping Tool"><b class="whb">Snipping Tool</b></a>.</b> The Snipping Tool is a great way to take all kinds of screenshots, including full-screen, individual windows, and even a particular area of the screen.<sup id="_ref-14" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 14"><a href="#_note-14">[14]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_14" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>On Windows 10, press the <b>Windows key</b>, type <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">snip</kbd>, and click <b>Snipping tool</b>.
<ul><li>While Microsoft once intended to replace Snipping Tool with an updated tool called Snip &amp; Sketch, that tool no longer receives updates.<sup id="_ref-15" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 15"><a href="#_note-15">[15]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden id="ts_popup_15" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Research source</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"></a>

</span>
</sup> Microsoft now recommends using Snipping Tool, not Snip &amp; Sketch, for capturing screenshots.<sup id="_ref-16" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 16"><a href="#_note-16">[16]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_16" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
</li></ul>
</li>
<li>On Windows 8.1, swipe in from the edge, select <b>Search</b>, type <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">snipping</kbd>, and then select <b>Snipping Tool</b>.</li>
<li>On Windows 7, click the Start menu, type <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">snipping</kbd>, and then click <b>Snipping Tool</b>.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_18"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-318">
<a name="step_4_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><picture id="394f968adff3f0a8d51d508ad01dd855"><source type="image/webp" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="545" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e7/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg.webp 460w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="545" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e7/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="545" srcset="/images/thumb/e/e7/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="545" srcset="/images/thumb/e/e7/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg 728w"></source><img alt="Step 2 Choose the shape of the Snip." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e7/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="344" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/e\/e7\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/e\/e7\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-16-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":344,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":545,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Choose the shape of the Snip.</b> "Rectangular Snip" is chosen by default. Click the Arrow button next to the Mode button to change the Snip shape:<sup id="_ref-17" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 17"><a href="#_note-17">[17]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_17" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>
<b>Free-form Snip</b> lets you draw any shape with your mouse. The area inside the shape will be snipped.</li>
<li>
<b>Rectangular Snip</b> lets you select a rectangular area, which will be snipped.</li>
<li>
<b>Window Snip</b> lets you choose a window to snip.</li>
<li>
<b>Full-screen Snip</b> snips the whole screen, including all windows (except the Snipping Tool window).</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_19"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-319">
<a name="step_4_3" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-18-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><picture 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="540" (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">3</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Create a new Snip.</b> Click the <b>New</b> button to start the selection. The screen will fade, and you can draw your Snip area, or select the window if you chose Window Snip. Release the mouse to take your screenshot.
<ul><li>If you had <b>Full-screen Snip</b> selected, your Snip will automatically be created once you click <b>New</b>.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_20"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-320">
<a name="step_4_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-19-Version-4.jpg" class="image"><picture 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="554" the Snip (optional)." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/4/40/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-19-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-19-Version-4.jpg" (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">4</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Annotate the Snip (optional).</b> Once you create the Snip, it will open in a new window. You can use the Pen tool to draw on it and the Highlight tool to draw attention to text.
<ul><li>The Erase tool will only erase annotations, not the screenshot itself.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_21"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-321">
<a name="step_4_5" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-20-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><picture 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="543" Snip." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/68/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-20-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-20-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="343" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">5</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Save the Snip.</b> Click the floppy disk icon to open the save dialog. Type in a name for the screenshot and change the "Save as type:" field if desired. You can now send the screenshot by email or put it on a website.
<ul><li>PNG is the default format in Windows 8 and later. The default format in earlier versions is JPG.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_22"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-322">
<a name="step_4_6" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-21-Version-2.jpg" class="image"><picture 460w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="552" 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="552" srcset="/images/thumb/3/36/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-21-Version-2.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-21-Version-2.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="552" Snip (optional)." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/36/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-21-Version-2.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-21-Version-2.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="349" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/3\/36\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-21-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-21-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/3\/36\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-21-Version-2.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-21-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":349,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":552,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">6</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Paste the Snip (optional).</b> By default, the Snip is copied to the clipboard when you create it. This means you can paste it into Paint or <a href="/Add-an-Image-in-Word" title="Add an Image in Word">Word</a>, much like you would with a full-screen screenshot. In Paint, you can make more edits than you can in the Snip annotation editor.
<ul><li>To paste the Snip, open a window that supports pasting and press <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">V</kbd></span>.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_23"></div>
</li>

<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-423">
<a name="step_5_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-24-Version-4.jpg" class="image"><picture class="whcdn" width="460" height="345" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Go to the view that you want to screenshot.</b> Open the program or screen you want to take a picture of, making sure that any windows or items you don't want on-screen are out of the way.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_24"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-424">
<a name="step_5_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg" class="image"><picture id="2512dabadfb00c39a14d31d250b35899"><source type="image/webp" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="546" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7d/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg.webp 460w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="546" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7d/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" srcset="/images/thumb/7/7d/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" srcset="/images/thumb/7/7d/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg 728w"></source><img alt="Step 2 Press  Win+ Shift+S." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7d/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="345" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/7\/7d\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/7\/7d\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-25-Version-4.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Press <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode"></span> Win</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode"></span> Shift</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">S</kbd></b></span>.</b> Doing so will cause your screen to turn grey, and your mouse will turn into a crosshairs icon. The Snipping Tool will open at the top of the screen.<sup id="_ref-18" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 18"><a href="#_note-18">[18]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_18" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
<ul>
<li>By default, the shortcut will open Snipping Tool in Rectangle Snip Mode, which means you can click and drag a rectangle around the area of the screen you want to capture.</li>
<li>On Windows 10, you can select a different screenshot mode from the <b>Mode</b> menu. For example, if you want to capture the whole screen, select <b>Full-screen Snip</b> (which takes the screenshot automatically). To capture a single window, select <b>Window Snip</b>.</li>
<li>On Windows 11, you can select a different mode to take a screenshot using the icons at the top. The icons in order are Rectangle (the default), Window, Full screen (which takes the screenshot automatically), and Freeform modes.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_25"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-425">
<a name="step_5_3" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg" class="image"><picture 460w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="546" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/39/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" srcset="/images/thumb/3/39/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" srcset="/images/thumb/3/39/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg 728w"></source><img alt="Step 3 Select an area to screenshot." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/39/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="345" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/3\/39\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/3\/39\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-26-Version-4.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">3</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Select an area to screenshot.</b> Click and drag your mouse from the top-left corner of the area you want to screenshot to the bottom-right corner. When you release the mouse button, the screenshot will be captured and copied to your clipboard.
<ul><li>If you selected a full-screen screenshot, you can skip this step.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_26"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-426">
<a name="step_5_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><picture id="6351b1b43e8a425784e018691cbafdc8"><source type="image/webp" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="546" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/85/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg.webp 460w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(max-width: 728px)" width="460" height="546" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/85/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg 460w"></source><source type="image/webp" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" srcset="/images/thumb/8/85/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg.webp 728w"></source><source type="image/jpeg" media="(min-width: 729px)" width="728" height="546" save your screenshot." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/85/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="345" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/8\/85\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/8\/85\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-27-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">4</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Paste or save your screenshot.</b> You can now paste your screenshot into any program that allows pasting photos (e.g., Paint, Word, an email, etc.) by pressing <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">V</kbd></span>. You should see the section of the screen that you selected appear in your program.
<ul><li>Alternatively, save your screenshot as an image file by pressing <b>Ctrl + S</b>, entering a name, selecting a save location, and clicking <b>Save</b>.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_27"></div>
</li>

<div class="method_label">Method 6 of 8:</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Take-a-Screenshot-of-a-Game-or-App">Take a Screenshot of a Game or App</span></h3>
</div>
<a class="large_pdf_link pdf_link  disabled  pdf_link_steps  " href="#">

<li id="step-id-527">
<a name="step_6_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter "><a href="#/Image:Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-28-Version-4.jpg" class="image"><picture Xbox Game Bar." src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/b0/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-28-Version-4.jpg/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-Step-28-Version-4.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="345" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a> (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Open the Xbox Game Bar.</b> The <a href="/Open-the-Xbox-Game-Bar" title="Open the Xbox Game Bar">Game Bar</a> is a handy tool that makes it easy to capture screenshots of games, as well as any other open windows on your PC. To open the tool, press <b>Windows key</b> + <b>G</b> at the same time.<sup id="_ref-19" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 19"><a href="#_note-19">[19]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_19" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
<ul><li>You can even use the Xbox Game Bar to <a href="/Record-Your-Screen-in-Windows-10" title="Record Your Screen in Windows 10">record your screen</a> in real time.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_28"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-528">

<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Click the Widget menu.</b> It's the second icon from the left in the Game Bar at the top of the screen.<sup id="_ref-20" class="reference" aria-label="Link to Reference 20"><a href="#_note-20">[20]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden id="ts_popup_20" style="display: none;">

<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">3</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Click <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><span class="nowrap" title="This is not a clickable button; it illustrates the button one should find." style="font-family:Lucida Sans Unicode,Lucida Grande,sans-serif;font-size:14px;padding:0em 1em; border:1px solid; border-color:#AAA #555 #555 #AAA; -moz-border-radius: 4px; -webkit-border-radius: 4px; border-radius: 4px; background-color: #F2F2F2; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #FCFCFC, #E0E0E0); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #FCFCFC, #E0E0E0); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #FCFCFC, #E0E0E0); background-image: linear-gradient(top, #FCFCFC, #E0E0E0);">Capture</span></b></span>.</b> You'll see this near the top of the menu. <ul><li>When you're finished taking screenshots, follow these steps to unpin the Capture widget:
<ul>
<li>Press <b>Windows key</b> + <b>G</b> to reopen the Game Bar.</li>
<li>Click the pushpin icon.</li>
<li>Click anywhere on the screen.</li>
</ul>

decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="345" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/thumb\/f\/fc\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-35-Version-2.jpg\/v4-460px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-35-Version-2.jpg","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/f\/fc\/Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-35-Version-2.jpg\/v4-728px-Take-a-Screenshot-in-Microsoft-Windows-%28Draft%29-Step-35-Version-2.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":728,"bigHeight":546,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>\u00a9 2025 wikiHow, Inc. This image may not be used by other entities without the express written consent of wikiHow, Inc.<br>\n<\/p><p><br \/>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Press and hold the Power and Volume Up buttons at the same time.</b> This quick shortcut will instantly screenshot the whole screen on a Surface Laptop, Surface Pro, Surface Book, Surface Go, or Surface Studio. The screen will dim momentarily to indicate a screenshot was taken. Your screenshot will be stored in the Screenshots folder, which you can access by <a href="/Open-File-Explorer" title="Open File Explorer">opening File Explorer</a> and navigating to <b>Pictures</b>  <b>Screenshots</b>.
<ul>
<li>If you have a Surface Duo 2, press and hold the Power and Volume Down buttons instead.</li>
<li>For more control over your screenshots, use the Snipping Tool instead.</li>
</ul>

class="whcdn" width="460" height="345" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script (screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Go to the initial screen you want to screenshot.</b> This should be the first page in the sequence of pages that you want to screenshot.
<ul>
<li>
<b>Understand how this works.</b> The Windows Steps Recorder allows you to record up to 100 different screens and save them all to one document. This program also makes a note of where you click and which actions you perform on each screen.</li>
<li>This tool is being phased out on Windows 11 beginning in 2024.<sup id="_ref-23" class="reference trusted" aria-label="Link to Reference 23"><a href="#_note-23">[23]</a><span class="ts_popup trustedsource" hidden id="ts_popup_23" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<a class="ts_trustworthy" href="/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience">Trustworthy Source</a>

		<span class="ts_name">Microsoft Support</span>
		<span class="ts_description">Technical support and product information from Microsoft.</span>

				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Go to source</a>
</span>
</sup>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_36"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-736">

(screenshot)<br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Open the Steps Recorder.</b> To do so, press the <b>Windows key</b> on your keyboard, type <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">psr.exe</kbd>, and press <b>Enter</b>.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="scrolltomarker" data-isstep="1" id="scrollto_marker_steps_37"></div>
</li>

Doing so turns on the Steps Recorder, which will record the next 25 screen changes.
<ul><li>If you want to record more than 25 changes, first click <div class="mwimg  t techicon floatright " style="max-width:128px"><a href="#/Image:Android7dropdown.png" class="image"><picture id="9301b138cf94c5e7f530584d207c65c8"><img alt="Android 7 Dropdown" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/8/82/Android7dropdown.png" decoding="async" class="whcdn" width="460" height="460" loading="lazy"></picture><div class="image_details"><script type="application/json">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images\/8\/82\/Android7dropdown.png","bigUrl":"\/images\/thumb\/8\/82\/Android7dropdown.png\/30px-Android7dropdown.png","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":460,"bigWidth":30,"bigHeight":30,"licensing":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\"><p>I edited this screenshot of an Android icon.\n<\/p><p>License: <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"http:\/\/en.wikipedia.org\/wiki\/Fair_use\">Fair Use<\/a><br>\n<\/p><\/div>"}</script></div></a></div> on the right side of the toolbar, click <b>Settings...</b>, and change the "Number of recent screen captures to store" number.</li></ul>

<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">4</div><div class="step">

<div class="step_num" aria-hidden="true">7</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb" aria-hidden="true">Save your screenshots to a ZIP folder.</b> Click <b>Save</b> at the top of the window, enter a file name, select a save location, and click <b>Save</b>.
<ul><li>This will save the screenshots in one HTML file. You can open the HTML file in your browser to view its contents.</li></ul>
</div>

			<ul id="qa_article_questions" class="qa_questions qa_aqs">
					<li id="qa_question_0" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="11647" data-cqid="11657" data-caid="12513" data-sqid="43369" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="98" data-votes_down="57" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="0">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">What versions of Windows include the Snipping Tool?</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_user_area">
								
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture>
										<source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/f/f2/CommunityAvatar3.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar3.png.webp"></source>
										<img src="/images/thumb/f/f2/CommunityAvatar3.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar3.png" width="52" height="52" class="qa_person_circle-img" loading="lazy" alt="Community Answer">
									</picture>
								</div>
				
								<div class="qa_answerer_info">
				
									<div class="qa_user_name"></div>
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Community Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								The Snipping Tool is included in all versions of Windows since Windows Vista. This includes Vista, 7, 8, 10, Server 2008, and Server 2012. The only versions of Windows that it is not included in are Windows 7 Starter and Windows 7 Home Basic. If you are using either of these two versions, you will need to find another utility for taking screenshots, or use the keyboard shortcuts.
							</div>
								<div class="qa_answer_footer">
									<div class="wh_vote_container qa_vote_buttons">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">

					<li id="qa_question_1" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="68796" data-cqid="68813" data-caid="69669" data-sqid="227272" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="67" data-votes_down="41" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="0">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">After I capture a screenshot, how do I create arrows and circles?</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_user_area">
								
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture>
										<source type="image/webp" srcset="/images/thumb/0/0a/CommunityAvatar1.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar1.png.webp"></source>
										<img src="/images/thumb/0/0a/CommunityAvatar1.png/-crop-104-104-104px-CommunityAvatar1.png" width="52" height="52" class="qa_person_circle-img" loading="lazy" alt="Community Answer">
									</picture>
								</div>
				
								<div class="qa_answerer_info">
				
									<div class="qa_user_name"></div>
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Community Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								You have to load your previous screenshot into a photo editing software (e.g., Adobe Photoshop, Picasa, or even MS Paint) to edit your photo. Then you can draw arrows/circles on your screenshot and save the picture.
							</div>
								<div class="qa_answer_footer">

					<li id="qa_question_2" class="qa_aq qa_block " data-aqid="229970" data-cqid="229987" data-caid="230843" data-sqid="303898" data-qa_inactive="0" data-votes_up="33" data-votes_down="29" data-verifier_id="0" data-submitter_id="1978392">
					<div class="qa_divider"></div>
				
					<div class="qa_li_container">
						<div class="qa_question_tab">Question</div>
						<div class="qa_q_txt">The screenshots came out fine, but the actual image came out distorted, for example drawers in a dresser appear "squished." What do I do?</div>
						
				
				
						<div class="qa_answers">
							<div class="qa_user_area">
								
				
								<div class="qa_user_hover hint_box">
										
										
								</div>
				
				
								<div class="qa_person_circle">
									<picture>
										<source type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.wikihow.com/images/avatarOut/f/f1/1978392.jpg?20130604034331.webp"></source>
										<img src="https://www.wikihow.com/images/avatarOut/f/f1/1978392.jpg?20130604034331" width="52" height="52" class="qa_person_circle-img" loading="lazy" alt="Anuj_Kumar1">
									</picture>
								</div>
				
								<div class="qa_answerer_info">
				
									<div class="qa_user_name"><span class="qa_user_link" data-href="/User:Anuj_Kumar1">Anuj_Kumar1</span></div>
				
									<div class="qa_user_label">Community Answer</div>
									
								</div>
							</div>
				
							<div class="qa_answer answer ">
								Try taking a screenshot at maximum possible resolution for getting good quality shots. Also, you may check the screenshot saving app for the maximum output quality setting. You can take high resolution screenshots in virtual machines (even greater resolution than your monitor screen).
							</div>
								<div class="qa_answer_footer">
