<div class="section tips sticky font_test">
<div class="headline_container  block_header">
<div class="altblock"></div>
<div class="headline_info"><h2 class="section-heading" onclick="javascript:mfTempOpenSection(3)">
<div class="mw-ui-icon mw-ui-icon-element indicator"></div>
<span class="mw-headline" id="Tips">Tips</span>
</h2></div>
</div>
<div id="tips" class="section_text">
<ul class="tips_section_text_ul">
<li class="tips_ul_li">
<div class="tips_li_div">For those with <a href="/Use-OneNote" title="Use OneNote">Microsoft OneNote</a>, pressing <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode"></span> Win</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">S</kbd></span> brings up the option to take a rectangular snip of the screen. Doing so causes the snapshot to appear as an image in OneNote.<div class="clearall tips_li_div"></div>
</div>
<div class="wh_vote_container tips_li_div">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks</span>
	<div class="tips_li_div">
		<a href="#" data-hash="f492744ffc2d2954eb50fab1ab627848" data-vote="up" data-type="1" class="trvote_up_f492744ffc2d2954eb50fab1ab627848_1 vote_up wh_vote_box">
			Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
		<a href="#" data-hash="f492744ffc2d2954eb50fab1ab627848" data-vote="down" data-type="1" class="trvote_down_f492744ffc2d2954eb50fab1ab627848_1 vote_down wh_vote_box">
			Not Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">1</span>
		</a>
	</div>
</div>


</li>
<li class="tips_ul_li">
<div class="tips_li_div">On laptop keyboards, the <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode"></span> PrtScr</kbd></span> key might be combined with another key. This means that you have to press the <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Fn</kbd></span> key or "Function" key to access it. Such a key is usually found on the bottom row of the keyboard.<div class="clearall tips_li_div"></div>
</div>
<div class="wh_vote_container tips_li_div">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks</span>
	<div class="tips_li_div">
		<a href="#" data-hash="86670eb13f749adb513a03b5084c850b" data-vote="up" data-type="1" class="trvote_up_86670eb13f749adb513a03b5084c850b_1 vote_up wh_vote_box">
			Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
		<a href="#" data-hash="86670eb13f749adb513a03b5084c850b" data-vote="down" data-type="1" class="trvote_down_86670eb13f749adb513a03b5084c850b_1 vote_down wh_vote_box">
			Not Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">1</span>
		</a>
	</div>
</div>


</li>
<li class="tips_ul_li">
<div class="tips_li_div">Most screenshots will not show the mouse cursor.<div class="clearall tips_li_div"></div>
</div>
<div class="wh_vote_container tips_li_div">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks</span>
	<div class="tips_li_div">
		<a href="#" data-hash="210046b5a5bc8b8dbc1ea9c6555cfa51" data-vote="up" data-type="1" class="trvote_up_210046b5a5bc8b8dbc1ea9c6555cfa51_1 vote_up wh_vote_box">
			Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">0</span>
		</a>
		<a href="#" data-hash="210046b5a5bc8b8dbc1ea9c6555cfa51" data-vote="down" data-type="1" class="trvote_down_210046b5a5bc8b8dbc1ea9c6555cfa51_1 vote_down wh_vote_box">
			Not Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">1</span>
		</a>
	</div>
</div>


</li>
</ul>

<div class="headline_info">
<span class="toc_item" data-label="" data-disabled="disabled"></span><h2 class="section-heading" onclick="javascript:mfTempOpenSection(4)">
<div class="mw-ui-icon mw-ui-icon-element indicator"></div>
<span class="mw-headline" id="Warnings">Warnings  </span>
</h2>
</div>
</div>
<div id="warnings" class="section_text">
<ul>
<li class="warnings_ul_li"><div class="warnings_li_div">Saving screenshots in some file types (such as bitmaps) will result in very large files. Because of this, it's highly recommended to use the PNG or JPEG format.<div class="clearall warnings_li_div"></div>
</div>
<div class="wh_vote_container warnings_li_div">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks</span>
	<div class="warnings_li_div">
		<a href="#" data-hash="191886058f0555ca8f4c9b66d4a0f8f0" data-vote="up" data-type="2" class="trvote_up_191886058f0555ca8f4c9b66d4a0f8f0_2 vote_up wh_vote_box">
			Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">4</span>
		</a>
		<a href="#" data-hash="191886058f0555ca8f4c9b66d4a0f8f0" data-vote="down" data-type="2" class="trvote_down_191886058f0555ca8f4c9b66d4a0f8f0_2 vote_down wh_vote_box">
			Not Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">2</span>
		</a>
	</div>
</div>


</li>
<li class="warnings_ul_li"><div class="warnings_li_div">DRM-protected content will not be visible in your screenshot and will be blanked out.<div class="clearall warnings_li_div"></div>
</div>
<div class="wh_vote_container warnings_li_div">
	<span class="wh_thumb_response wh_thumb_msg">Thanks</span>
	<div class="warnings_li_div">
		<a href="#" data-hash="64425f63001143967dd95f9809c5a9c3" data-vote="up" data-type="2" class="trvote_up_64425f63001143967dd95f9809c5a9c3_2 vote_up wh_vote_box">
			Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">5</span>
		</a>
		<a href="#" data-hash="64425f63001143967dd95f9809c5a9c3" data-vote="down" data-type="2" class="trvote_down_64425f63001143967dd95f9809c5a9c3_2 vote_down wh_vote_box">
			Not Helpful
			<span class="tr_vote">3</span>

<a href="#_ref-23" target="_blank"></a> <span class="reference-text"><a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" class="external free" href="https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/steps-recorder-deprecation-a64888d7-8482-4965-8ce3-25fb004e975f">https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/steps-recorder-deprecation-a64888d7-8482-4965-8ce3-25fb004e975f</a></span>

</ol></div></div>
